    The value is undefined.

  • When used in any other admissible structural element (group or unit):

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingScoreThreshold property of its parent element (which can be undefined).

  • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingScoreThreshold property of the innermost <mrk>, unit, or mtc_matches array element in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

  • When used in the <mtc_matches array element:

    The value is undefined.

Warning

The its_locQualityRatingScoreThreshold property is intended to be used in concert with the its_locQualityRatingProfileRef property that is to provide information on the applicable Quality Assessment Model. Without providing quality assessment model information behind the acceptance threshold, the score between 0 and 100 is very likely to be useless and not interoperable.

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, and sm.

See the ITS Localization Quality Rating Annotation for the normative usage description of this property when used inline; advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

See Localization Quality Rating on Structural Elements for advanced Constraints when used on strcutural elements (file, group, and unit).

See Localization Quality Rating in Translation Candidates Module for advanced Constraints when used within the Translation Candidates Module.

5.9.12.17 its_locQualityRatingVote

Localization Quality Rating Vote - the its_locQualityRatingVote property is the [ITS] defined its_locQualityRatingVote property.

This property provides the quality rating voting (crowd assessment) results pertaining to a structural or inline portion of target text, the higher the number the more positive votes or the better margin of positive votes over negative votes. Tools are expected to interpret this value within their own quality rating system.

Type: integer.

Value description: an integer value.

Default value: default values for this property depend on the object in which it is used:

  • When used in file:

    The value is undefined.

  • When used in any other admissible structural element (group or unit):

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingVote property of its parent object (which can be undefined).

  • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingVote property of the innermost <mrk>, unit, or mtc_matches array element in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

  • When used in the mtc_matches array element:

    The value is undefined.

Warning

The its_locQualityRatingVote property is intended to be used in concert with the its_locQualityRatingScoreThreshold property, that encodes the vote's success or failure criteria and ideally also the its_locQualityRatingProfileRef property that is to provide information on the applicable Quality Assessment Model. Without providng a success threshold or quality assessment model information, the integer encoding the voting (crowd assessment) results is very likely to be useless and not interoperable.

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, sm, and mtc_matches array elements.

See the ITS Localization Quality Rating Annotation for the normative usage description of this attribute when used inline; advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

See Localization Quality Rating on Structural Elements for advanced Constraints when used on strcutural elements (file, group, and unit).

See Localization Quality Rating in Translation Candidates Module for advanced Constraints when used within the Translation Candidates Module.

5.9.12.18 its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold

Localization Quality Rating Vote Threshold - the its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property is the [ITS] defined its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property.

This property provides the minimum passing vote threshold for any Localization Quality Rating Votes that are in scope of the its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property.

Type: integer.

Value description: an integer value.

Default value: default values for this property depend on the object in which it is used:

  • When used in file:

    The value is undefined.

  • When used in any other admissible structural element (group or unit):

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property of its parent object (which can be undefined).

  • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

    The value of the its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property of the innermost <mrk>, unit or mtc_matches array element in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

  • When used in the mtc_matches array element:

    The value is undefined.

Warning

The its_locQualityRatingVoteThreshold property is intended to be used in concert with the its_locQualityRatingProfileRef attribute that is to provide information on the applicable Quality Assessment Model. Without providng the quality assessment model information, the voting threshold integer is very likely to be useless and not interoperable.

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, sm, and mtc_matches array elements.

See the ITS Localization Quality Rating Annotation for the normative usage description of this property when used inline; advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

See Localization Quality Rating on Structural Elements for advanced Constraints when used on strcutural elements (file, group, and unit).

See Localization Quality Rating in Translation Candidates Module for advanced Constraints when used within the Translation Candidates Module.

5.9.12.19 its_mtConfidence

Machine Translation Confidence - the its_mtConfidence property is the [ITS] defined its_mtConfidence property.

Type: number.

Value description: a floating point number between 0.0 and 1.0, inclusive.

The number represents the self-reported confidence of the application or service providing the MT Confidence metadata, the higher the better.

Default value:: undefined.

Used in: <mrk>, and sm.

Constraints

  • When the property its_mtConfidence is set, the element where it is set MUST be in the scope of an its_annotatorsRef property with the [ITS]Data category identifier part of exactly one list value equal to the string "mt-confidence".

See the ITS MT Confidence Annotation for the full normative usage description of this property. Other advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

Processing Requirements

  • Writers MUST use the mtc_matchQuality property to express the MTConfidence property on an mtc_matches array element.

    • The floating point number between 0.0 and 1.0 MUST be expressed as a percentage decimal number between 0.0 and 100.0 [%].

    • The mtc_matchQuality property used by the Writer to express the MTConfidence property MUST be in scope of an its_annotatorsRef property with the [ITS]Data category identifier part of exactly one list value equal to the string "mt-confidence".

  • Modifiers MAY use this MTConfidence property, when populating the XLIFF Core target elements with exact unmodified MT matches from mtc_matches array elements with the mtc_matchQuality property set and in scope of an its_annotatorsRef property with the [ITS]Data category identifier part of exactly one list value equal to the string "mt-confidence".

    • The percentage decimal number between 0.0 and 100.0 [%] MUST be expressed as a floating point number between 0.0 and 1.0.

5.9.12.20 its_org

Organization - the its_org attribute is the [ITS] defined its_org property.

Type: string.

Value description: text.

The text string is supposed to identify an organizational translation agent as per Organizational provenance information.

Default value: default values for this property depend on the element in which it is used:

  • When used in any admissible element WITH the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The value of the its_org property of the first its_provenanceRecords array element with the its_org property set within the referenced its_provenanceRecords property (which can be undefined).

  • When used in any admissible element WITHOUT the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The default values depending on the object in which it is used:

    • When used in file or its_provencanceRecords array element:

      The value is undefined.

    • When used in any other admissible structural element (group or unit):

      The value of the its_org property of its parent object (which can be undefined).

    • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

      The value of the its_org property of the innermost <mrk>, unit, mtc_matches array element, or ctr_revision element, in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, sm, its_provenanceRecords array elements, mtc_matches array elements, and ctr_revision object.

See the ITS Provenance Annotation for the normative usage description of this property on inline elements. Advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

5.9.12.24 its_provenanceRecordsRef

Provenance Records Standoff Reference - the its_provenanceRecordsRef property is the [ITS] defined its_provenanceRecordsRef property.

This property references the collection of Provenance Records that pertain to the content span or structural element content from where the reference is declared.

Type: string.

Value description: IRI.

Default value: undefined.

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, sm, mtc_matches array elements, and ctr_revision.

See the ITS Localization Issue Annotation for the normative usage description of this property inline.

Constraints

  • Multiple its_provenanceRecordsRef properties MAY reference the same its_provenanceRecords array elements.

  • In case the its_provenanceRecordsRef property is used on a n <mrk> or sm object,

    • The value of the its_provenanceRecordsRef property MUST be an IRI referencing a its_provenanceRecords array element within the innermost enclosing unit, mtc_matches array element, or ctr_revisionobject.

  • In case the its_provenanceRecordsRef property is used on a file, group, or unit object,

    • The value of the its_provenanceRecordsRef property MUST be an IRI referencing a its_provenanceRecords array element within the same object or its ancestor object.

Processing Requirements

  • Modifiers removing the last its_provenanceRecordsRef property referencing a its_provenanceRecords array MUST delete that its_provenanceRecords array element.

Used in: <mrk>, and <sm>.

Constraints

  • When the property its_taSource is set, the its_taIdent property MUST be set as well.

See the ITS Text Analysis Annotation for the full normative usage description of this property. Other advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

5.9.12.36 its_termConfidence

Terminology Confidence - the its_termConfidence property is the [ITS] defined its_termConfidence property.

Type: number.

Value description: floating point number between 0.0 and 10, inclusive.

The number represents the self reported confidence of the application or service providing the Terminology metadata, the higher the better.

Default value:: undefined.

Used in: <mrk>, and sm.

Constraints

  • When the property its_termConfidence is set, the element where it is set MUST be in the scope of an its_annotatorsRef property with the [ITS]Data category identifier part of exactly one list value equal to the string "terminology".

See the ITS Terminology Annotation for the full normative usage description of this property. Other advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

5.9.12.37 its_tool

Tool - the its_tool property is the [ITS] defined its_tool property.

Type: string.

Value description: text.

The text string is supposed to identify a software tool translation agent as per Tool-related provenance information.

Default value: default values for this property depend on the object in which it is used:

  • When used in any admissible object WITH the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The value of the its_tool property of the first its_provenanceRecords array element with the its_tool property set within the referenced its_provenanceRecords array (which can be undefined).

  • When used in any admissible element WITHOUT the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The default values depening on the object in which it is used:

    • When used in file or its_provencanceRecords array element:

      The value is undefined.

    • When used in any other admissible structural object (group or unit):

      The value of the its_tool property of its parent object (which can be undefined).

    • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

      The value of the its_tool property of the innermost <mrk>, unit, mtc_matches array element, or ctr_revision object element, in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

Used in: file, group, unit, <mrk>, sm, its_provenanceRecords array element, mtc_matches array element, and ctr_revision object.

See the ITS Provenance Annotation for the normative usage description of this property on inline elements. Advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

5.9.12.38 its_toolRef

Tool Reference - the its_toolRef property is the [ITS] defined its_toolRef property.

Type: string.

Value description: IRI.

The IRI is supposed to resolve as human or machine readable Tool-related provenance information.

Default value: default values for this property depend on the element in which it is used:

  • When used in any admissible object WITH the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The value of the its_toolRef property of the first its_provenanceRecords array element with the its_toolRef property set within the referenced its_provenanceRecord> array (which can be undefined).

  • When used in any admissible object WITHOUT the its_provenanceRecordsRef property set:

    The default values depening on the object in which it is used:

    • When used in file or its_provencanceRecords array element:

      The value is undefined.

    • When used in any other admissible structural object (group or unit):

      The value of the its_toolRef property of its parent object (which can be undefined).

    • When used in annotations markers <mrk> or sm:

      The value of the its_toolRef property of the innermost <mrk>, unit, mtc_matches array element, or ctr_revision object element, in which the marker in question is located (which can be undefined).

Used in: file, group, <unit>, <mrk>, sm, its_provenanceRecords array element, mtc_matches array element, and ctr_revision object.

See the ITS Provenance Annotation for the normative usage description of this property on inline elements. Advanced Constraints follow from that normative usage description.

5.9.13 Example file

Example 28. ITS Data Categories Example

The following example file includes markup related to several ITS 2.0 data categories.

<!-- xliff-its-example.xlf: Example file that shows several features of
using ITS 2.0 as part of XLIFF 2.1
Version: 0.2.1 
Date: 04 April 2017 -->

<xliff version="2.1" xmlns="urn:oasis:names:tc:xliff:document:2.0"
    srcLang="en" trgLang="fr"
    xmlns:its="http://www.w3.org/2005/11/its" xmlns:itsm="urn:oasis:names:tc:xliff:itsm:2.1">
  <!-- Each unit in the file element shows one ITS data category. -->
  <!-- The its:annotatorsRef attribute inherits through the whole file
      but is only relevant for some elements-->
  <file id="f1" its:annotatorsRef="allowed-characters|
      http://example.com/myAllowedCharactersAnnotationTool terminology|
      http://example.com/mytermTool localization-quality-issue|
      http://example.com/anotherQualityChecker">
    <unit id="u1">
      <its:locQualityIssues xml:id="lqi1">
        <its:locQualityIssue locQualityIssueType="misspelling"
            locQualityIssueComment="'c'es' is unknown. Could be 'c'est'"
            locQualityIssueSeverity="50"/>
        <its:locQualityIssue locQualityIssueType="grammar"
            locQualityIssueComment="Sentence is not capitalized"
            locQualityIssueSeverity="30"/>
      </its:locQualityIssues>
      <its:provenanceRecords xml:id="prov1">
        <its:provenanceRecord revPerson="Franta Kocourek"
            revOrg="Kocourkov s.r.o."/>
        <its:provenanceRecord person="Honza Novák"
            org="Překlady Novák, sro" tool="GreatCATTool"/>
        <its:provenanceRecord tool="Microsoft Hub"/>
      </its:provenanceRecords>
      <its:provenanceRecords xml:id="prov2">
        <its:provenanceRecord revPerson="Květoň Zřídkaveselý"
            revOrg="CoolCopy"/>
        <its:provenanceRecord revTool="ACME QA Checker"
            revOrg="CoolCopy"/>
        <its:provenanceRecord revPerson="Franta Kocourek"
            revOrg="Kocourkov s.r.o."/>
        <its:provenanceRecord person="Honza Novák"
            org="Preklady Novák, sro" tool="GreatCATTool"/>
        <its:provenanceRecord tool="Microsoft Hub"/>
      </its:provenanceRecords>
      <notes>
        <note id="1" priority="1">Check with terminology engineer
            </note>
      </notes>

      <!-- Example for allowed characters data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>
          <mrk id="m1" type="its:generic"
              its:allowedCharacters="[a-ZA-Z]">Text</mrk>
        </source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for domain data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>Text in the domain domain1</source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for locale filter data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>Text <pc id="2"><mrk id="m2" type="its:generic"
            its:localeFilterList="fr" its:localeFilterType="exclude">
            text</mrk></pc></source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for localization quality issue data category. The
          standoff information in its:locQualityIssues has the
          annotatorsRef information from this element: <mrk id="m1"
          type="its:generic" its:locQualityIssuesRef="#its=lqi1"
          its:annotatorsRef="localization-quality-issue|
          http://example.com/myQualityChecker">.  -->

      <segment>
        <source>This is the content</source>
        <target>
          <mrk id="m3" type="its:generic" its:locQualityIssuesRef="#its=lqi1"
              its:annotatorsRef="localization-quality-issue|
              http://example.com/myQualityChecker">c'es le contenu</mrk>
        </target>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for localization quality rating data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>Some text and a term</source>
        <target>Du texte et un <mrk id="m4" type="its:generic"
            its:locQualityRatingVote="37"
            its:locQualityRatingVoteThreshold="15"
            its:locQualityRatingProfileRef="http://example.org/qaModel
                /v13">terme</mrk></target>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for text analytics data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>
          <mrk id="m5" type="its:generic"
              its:taClassRef="http://nerd.eurecom.fr/ontology#Place"
              its:taIdentRef="http://dbpedia.org/resource/Arizona">
              Arizona</mrk>
        </source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for terminology data category, expressed via native XLIFF markup -->

      <segment>
        <source>This is a <mrk id="m6" type="comment" ref="#n=1">
            motherboard</mrk>.</source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for terminology data category, expressed via native XLIFF markup, but with its:termConfidence attribute -->

      <segment>
        <source>Text with a <pc id="3"><mrk id="m7" type="term"
            ref="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terminology"
            its:termConfidence="0.9">term</mrk></pc>.</source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for language information data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>Span of text <pc id="4"><mrk id="m8" itsm:lang="fr"
            type="its:generic">en français</mrk></pc>.</source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for provenance information data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>Economy has been growing in 2016.</source>
        <target>
          <mrk id="m9" type="its:generic"
              its:provenanceRecordsRef="#its=prov1">Hospodářství v průbehu
              roku 2016 rostlo. </mrk>
        </target>
      </segment>
      <segment>
        <source>Prognosis for 2017 is unclear.</source>
        <target>
           <mrk id="m10" type="its:generic"
               its:provenanceRecordsRef="#its=prov2">Předpověď očekávaného růstu
               pro rok 2017 je nejasná. </mrk>
        </target>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for MT confidence data category -->

      <segment>
        <source>
          <mrk id="m11" type="its:generic" its:mtConfidence="0.8982"
              its:annotatorsRef="mt-confidence|MTServices-XYZ">Some
              Machine Translated text.</mrk>
        </source>
      </segment>

      <!-- Example for Translate data category, expressed via native XLIFF markup -->

      <segment>
        <source><mrk translate="no" id="m12">Non-translatable text
            </mrk></source>
      </segment>

    </unit>
  </file>
</xliff>
